# UCL vs local CPOSS HTML consistency audit (pre-synchronization snapshot)

Generated 6 July 2026 before the subsequent UCL-content synchronization. This report preserves the discrepancies that existed at audit time and is not a description of the current synchronized files.

## Scope and comparison rules

- Remote source: `https://www.chem.ucl.ac.uk/cposs/database/molecule_list2.html` and its 49 linked molecule pages.
- Local source: the uniquely matching generated `.html` file in this repository.
- The legacy UCL navigation banner, footer, CSS, and heading-level differences are excluded as presentation-only.
- Page headings, update dates, prose/captions, table structure and every differing table cell, content images, downloadable resources, and DOI links are compared.
- “Remote only” and “Local only” are directional: they do not automatically indicate which version is correct.

## Executive summary

- Pages: 49
- Title mismatches: 35
- Pages with prose diffs: 49
- Pages with table diffs: 49
- Pages with image diffs: 23
- Pages with resource diffs: 49
- Pages with doi diffs: 47
- Total table cell or structure diffs: 2798

## 2-chlorobenzamide

- Remote: `2chlorobenzamide.html`

  - Remote only: Figure 1. The molecular diagram of 2-chlorobenzamide.
  - Local only: Figure . The molecular diagram of 2-chlorobenzamide.

  - Remote only: Figure 2. Lattice Energy Landscapes of 2chlorobenzamide. Energy models B1,C1,A1.
  - Local only: Figure . Crystal energy landscape of 2-chlorobenzamide from previous work. Top: from Study_ID=10. Bottom left: from Study_ID=0. Bottom right: from Study_ID=2.
- **replace:**
  - Remote only: Table 1. Crystallographic information and experimental information of CSD entries for 2chlorobenzamide. Different polymorphs, as ascertained by structure matching of 20 molecule coordination sphere in Mercury, are coloured differently. Reference polymorphs are outlined in bold.
  - Local only: Table . Crystallographic information for CSD entries for 2-chlorobenzamide. Different polymorphs are coloured differently.

  - Local only: Two other polymorphs of 2-chlorobenzamide are reported, CLBZAM02 gamma and CLBZMA03 delta. Neither have space groups or full structures.
  - Local only: Table . Experimental information for CSD entries for XXX.

  - Local only: Other notes

  - Local only: The chlorine potential was different in the case of Anastasia's search. The cross term was consistent (within rounding errors in Excel). The cross potential used by Bob's search was wrong.

- **replace:**
  - Remote only: Figure 2. Lattice Energy Landscapes of Olanzapine. Energy models A3,B2.

  - Remote only: Table 1. Crystallographic information and experimental information of CSD entries for Olanzapine. Different polymorphs, as ascertained by structure matching of 20 molecule coordination sphere in Mercury, are coloured differently. Reference polymorphs are outlined in bold.
  - Remote only: Crystallization conditions are included in the downloadable Word Document.
  - Remote only: Other Notes
  - Remote only: The study was originally done with two conformational regions named eq(uatorial) and ax(ial) relating to the manner in which the benzodiazepine group linked to the nitrogen atom. Susan Reutzel-Edens was not happy with these terms being used for a nitrogen atom, so they were changed to A and B respectively. (A is the conformation seen in the experimental crystal structures and is the lower in energy.) Crystal structures have been given to other groups with the old names, and hence these are occasionally referred to in the literature.
  - Remote only: A162 was originally thought to be the best match for form III, although Rajni Miglani Bhardwaj noted that there were problems with it and it was not perfect which is why it is referred to it as a model for form III in that paper.
  - Local only: Figure . Crystal energy landscape of Olanzapine from previous work. Top left, energy model 1 (CrystalPredictor search), bottom left, energy model 2 (CrystalOptimizer refinement), right, energy model 3 (rigid molecule refinement within PCM). Free energy approximations are also available for energy model 3 - see the spreadsheet.
  - Local only: CSD structures (CSD version 5.45 with Mar, Jun and Sep 2024 updates)
  - Local only: Table . Crystallographic information for CSD entries for Olanzapine. Different polymorphs are coloured differently.
  - Local only: Table . Experimental information for CSD entries for Olanzapine.
  - Local only: Other notes
  - Local only: The study was originally done with two conformational regions named eq(uatorial) and ax(ial) relating to the manner in which the benzodiazepine group linked to the nitrogen atom. Susan Reutzel-Edenswas not happy with these terms being used for a nitrogen atom, so they were changed to A and B respectively. (A is the conformation seen in the experimental crystal structures and is the lower in energy.) Crystal structures have been given to other groups with the old names, and hence these are occasionally referred to in the literature.
  - Local only: A162 was originally thought to be the best match for form III, although Rajni Miglani Bhardwaj noted that there were problems with it and it wasn't perfect which it is referred to it as a model for form III in that paper.4
